Normally, Google Chrome updates automatically. If you still need to update your browser to watch Sling TV, open Google Chrome. \u00a0</p><p dir=\"ltr\">In the top-right corner, click on the Settings icon.</p><p dir=\"ltr\"><a href=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/4YvyHMA-n1mNsA0uo31mUA2YLIwS-ljUWhJ3dcgT6qaQ5JeE8o4DM3wGE5hJ1bY3s0DEHcge18eZ7-uQTFXeea13kxmtdi8Uv9Ex4eKsz13ZgfKzkk9EG-PtIxJL2vjw7Veh66m7\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><img src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/4YvyHMA-n1mNsA0uo31mUA2YLIwS-ljUWhJ3dcgT6qaQ5JeE8o4DM3wGE5hJ1bY3s0DEHcge18eZ7-uQTFXeea13kxmtdi8Uv9Ex4eKsz13ZgfKzkk9EG-PtIxJL2vjw7Veh66m7\" style=\"width: 624px; height: 341px;\" class=\"fr-dii\" alt=\"image of google home page on chrome browser with menu highlighted\"></a><br><br>Then click Update Google Chrome. If you do not see this option, this means you are on the latest version.</p><p dir=\"ltr\">Finally, click relaunch.</p><p dir=\"ltr\">To learn how to see what version of Google Chrome you are using, click <a href=\"/support/solutions/articles/33000219672-how-do-i-check-if-i-m-using-the-most-recent-version-of-google-chrome-\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>.</p></div><h4><strong>iOS Device</strong></h4><div><p>To check for, or install, an update temporarily leave the Sling TV app, then open your<span>\u00a0</span><em>App Store</em>.</p><p><br></p><p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-fil\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000548/original/ap_Wp2QhV-ZNNvF2bgOQtydy-DieWZHDTQ.png?1532024673\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000548/original/ap_Wp2QhV-ZNNvF2bgOQtydy-DieWZHDTQ.png?1532024673\" data-fileid=\"46000000548\" data-uniquekey=\"1532023399954\" style=\"width: 498px; height: 374.504px;\" alt=\"image of iOS home screen with app store highlighted\"></p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p>Look to the bottom right corner of your App Store to locate the<span>\u00a0</span><em>Updates</em><span>\u00a0</span>folder.</p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-fil\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000549/original/-_f4pbVetknajKk5ihxcmTlbZRE8U9sUcA.png?1532024754\" style=\"width: 496px; height: 372px;\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000549/original/-_f4pbVetknajKk5ihxcmTlbZRE8U9sUcA.png?1532024754\" data-fileid=\"46000000549\" data-uniquekey=\"1532023399954\" alt=\"image of app store with updates highlighted\"></p><p><br></p><p>If an update is available for Sling TV it will be listed here. Bandwidth","type":"ARTICLE","url":"/en/support/solutions/articles/33000219098-what-is-bandwidth-and-how-do-i-check-my-current-bandwidth-usage-","source":{"article":{"art_type":null,"created_at":"2018-03-01T12:28:22-07:00","desc_un_html":"  Bandwidth is the rate at which data can be transmitted from the internet to your device. The higher your bandwidth, the more usage you can have at the same time. For example, if you are currently streaming ESPN on Sling TV through your Roku Device while your roommate is streaming HGTV on the XBOX One through their Sling TV account you may notice a slight lag in streaming. The reason being, more bandwidth is being used to provide both of you with video content.     Try testing your internet speed here. Check for download speed,\u00a0or how fast you can pull in data with your connection. Make sure your speed is equal to or greater than the recommendations available below:     What internet speed do I need to stream Sling TV?    Constant speed of 3.0 Megabits per second (Mb/s) or more - Streaming video content on portable devices such as tablets or phones  Constant speed of 5.0 Mb/s or more - Single stream of video content on a TV, PC, or Mac  Constant speed of 25 Mb/s or more - Recommended for households that maintain internet usage on multiple devices       If your internet service provider (ISP) has a cap on your data, it's a good idea to keep an eye on your usage while streaming.\u00a0     Find out to check bandwidth usage below. Note that this setting is not available on all devices at this time.     Roku, Amazon, Android Mobile, Google Play, Google Chrome, iOS\u00a0   Visit the Connection page, located within your\u00a0SETTINGS,\u00a0to find your current streaming speed. \u00a0    Beneath your bandwidth control options you will see Current Bandwidth. The speed displayed is constantly charted based on the feed received from your ISP. If your streaming speed is impacting your available bandwidth, try settings controls on the speed allotted here. \u00a0Make the best of your streaming experience and control your bandwidth. \u00a0  XBOX One  Launch your SETTINGS, then Bandwidth Limiting\u00a0to locate your current streaming speed. The speed displayed is constantly charted based on the feed received from your ISP. If your streaming speed is impacting your available bandwidth, try settings controls on the speed allotted here. \u00a0Make the best of your streaming experience and control your bandwidth.      ","description":"<div id=\"pkb-accordion\"><p style=\"\">Bandwidth is the rate at which data can be transmitted from the internet to your device. The higher your bandwidth, the more usage you can have at the same time. For example, if you are currently streaming ESPN on Sling TV through your Roku Device while your roommate is streaming HGTV on the XBOX One through their Sling TV account you may notice a slight lag in streaming. The reason being, more bandwidth is being used to provide both of you with video content.</p><p><br></p><p>Try testing your internet speed <a href=\"http://www.speedtest.net/\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>. Check for <strong>download speed,\u00a0</strong>or how fast you can pull in data with your connection. Make sure your speed is equal to or greater than the recommendations available below:</p><p><br></p><h4><strong>What internet speed do I need to stream Sling TV?</strong></h4><div><ul><li>Constant speed of 3.0 Megabits per second (Mb/s) or more - Streaming video content on portable devices such as tablets or phones</li><li>Constant speed of 5.0 Mb/s or more - Single stream of video content on a TV, PC, or Mac</li><li>Constant speed of 25 Mb/s or more - Recommended for households that maintain internet usage on multiple devices</li></ul></div><p><br></p><p>If your internet service provider (ISP) has a cap on your data, it's a good idea to keep an eye on your usage while streaming.\u00a0</p><p><br></p><p>Find out to check bandwidth usage below. <em>Note that this setting is not available on all devices at this time.</em></p><p><br></p><h4><strong>Roku, Amazon, Android Mobile, Google Play, Google Chrome, iOS</strong>\u00a0</h4><div><p>Visit the <em>Connection</em> page, located within your<span>\u00a0</span><em>SETTINGS,\u00a0</em>to find your current streaming speed. \u00a0</p><p><br></p>Beneath your bandwidth control options you will see C<em>urrent Bandwidth</em>. The speed displayed is constantly charted based on the feed received from your ISP. If your streaming speed is impacting your available bandwidth, try settings controls on the speed allotted here. \u00a0Make the best of your streaming experience and control your bandwidth. <img alt=\"User-added image\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/33007729381/original/xLdct8WZnQSMnOzZ_zIF4bekQx5UWMKB1Q.png?1521227147\" style=\"width: 500px; height: 281px;\" class=\"fr-dii fr-draggable\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/33007729381/original/xLdct8WZnQSMnOzZ_zIF4bekQx5UWMKB1Q.png?1521227147\" data-fileid=\"33007729381\" data-uniquekey=\"1521226271144\">\u00a0</div><h4><strong>XBOX One</strong></h4><div>Launch your <em>SETTINGS</em>, then <em>Bandwidth Limiting\u00a0</em>to locate your current streaming speed. Amazon Fire TV        To download the Sling TV app on your Amazon Fire TV, follow the steps below.  Start by returning to your Amazon Fire TV home page, then click on the search icon in the upper-left corner of the screen.\u00a0                                                       Next, use the search engine to locate the Sling TV app by typing in Sling TV.  \u00a0                                                       You'll notice related titles will populate below the\u00a0Text Search\u00a0keyboard. Select Sling TV, or Sling Television, to locate the application.                                                          Click on the Sling TV application to open information about the app, as well as, begin the installation process.                                                          Now click\u00a0Download.                                                             Allow the download and installation process to run its course.                                                                                                                  Once the installation process is complete, click\u00a0Open\u00a0to launch the Sling TV app.                                                          Now it is time to enjoy your subscription! Sign in using your Sling TV account and enjoy! Sling TV should populate on the top of your list. \u00a0Click on Sling Television.                                                                                                                                              Next, click Download.                                                                                                                                              Allow the download and installation process to run its course.                                                                                                                                              Once the download is complete, click Open\u00a0to launch the Sling TV app! Sign in with your Sling TV account. If you do not have a Sling TV account, learn how to create one\u00a0here. Next, use the search engine to locate the Sling TV app.                                                                                                                                                 After opening Sling TV in the Google Play Store, click INSTALL to start the installation process. Allow the download and installation process to run its course.                                                                                                                                                 Once the installation is complete, press\u00a0OPEN\u00a0to launch the Sling TV app.                                                                                                                                                 Now that you have downloaded the Sling TV app, it is time to sign in. \u00a0If you do not have a Sling TV account, learn how to sign up\u00a0here. Chromecast   To setup your Chromecast device to work with Sling TV, follow the steps below.     To start, plug your Chromecast into your TV via an HDMI Port. \u00a0In order to power your device connect the USB power cable into the back end of your Chromecast. \u00a0Plug the opposite end into your nearest power source, or into any available USB port on your TV.     Now that your Chromecast device is plugged in to your TV, let's start by downloading the Google Home app to your mobile device or tablet.                                                                                                                                              Launch the Google Home app on your mobile device or tablet, then select the name of your Chromecast device.                                                                                                                                              Next, make sure the code on your TV matches the code displayed on your mobile device or tablet.                                                                                                                                                                                                Now its time to name your Chromecast device. Now that you have finished downloading your Sling TV app it is time to sign in and enjoy! If you do not have a Sling TV account, learn how to sign up\u00a0here. These can include work computers, devices at a friend\u2019s house, or any device that other users might have access to.  To sign out, start by selecting the Settings\u00a0icon in your Sling TV app. Note:\u00a0Depending on your device, this may appear as a gear icon, or as\u00a0SETTINGS in the top ribbon.     Next, scroll down to Account,\u00a0then select Sign Out.\u00a0       Important Note:\u00a0If you're a former Sling TV customer, to avoid accidentally restarting your subscription, make sure to sign out of your account if it's not in use. To find this option, on your Roku, Amazon or Android device, select\u00a0Browse Free Shows\u00a0(or\u00a0Rent Movies\u00a0on your Samsung, LG, XBOX One, Window 10 or browser player). You'll be taken to a menu similar to what you'd see with an active Sling TV account. Follow the instructions above to sign out.      Sign Out of all Devices     You can sign out of all devices currently using your account by logging in at sling.com. Find this option under the Personal Information\u00a0section of your My Account page.    Go to My Account      Passwords   Update your password periodically. Your password is your gateway to Sling TV, so let's keep it safe! When creating your password, we recommend you keep these key points in mind:   Your password must be between 4-30 characters  The longer the password, the stronger it will be. Use more characters to your advantage when building a unique password  Make sure your password is one-of-a-kind to your Sling TV account  Mix and match numbers, symbols, upper- and lowercase letters  Update your password   Forgot your password? No worries! Get instructions on how to reset it.      Virus Protection   Make sure your device\u2019s malware and virus protection software is up to date.       Finally, use the Contact Us\u00a0link at the very bottom of this page to reach out to us to report any fraudulent or suspicious activity, or if you believe someone else may have access to your Sling TV account. We\u2019re looking to add this","type":"ARTICLE","url":"/en/support/solutions/articles/46000000257-how-do-i-activate-the-sling-tv-app-on-my-device-","source":{"article":{"art_type":null,"created_at":"2019-04-10T10:02:31-06:00","desc_un_html":"   Note:\u00a0App activation is currently available on Samsung Smart TVs and will be available in the coming weeks on LG TV and XBOX One devices. We\u2019re looking to add this feature to more devices in the future.     If you\u2019re just looking for the link to authenticate Sling TV on your device, visit sling.com/activate\u00a0in your browser on mobile or desktop.     To activate the Sling TV app on your device, start by launching the app. From the landing page, if you already have a Sling TV subscription, select Sign In.\u00a0If you\u2019d like to start a Sling TV subscription, select Watch 7 Days FREE!          You\u2019ll see a screen with a five-digit code. From your smartphone, tablet or computer, visit sling.com/activate, or click here\u00a0(page will open in a new window).     Important Note:\u00a0Do NOT\u00a0use the code in the picture below. Use the code from your screen.             Enter your code in the text box, then select Continue.          For the next step, choose whether you\u2019re signing up for Sling TV, or signing in on your device:      I\u2019m signing up for Sling TV      \u00a0The next screen you\u2019ll see will ask you to choose what type of entertainment you\u2019re looking for. Select the drop-down menu to choose from US programming, Latino programming, or International programming in a number of languages. Once you\u2019ve made your pick, select Continue.              From here, you\u2019ll enter your email address and a unique password to create your account. Next, you\u2019ll select your programming, add any available extras you want and enter your payment information to complete signup.     For more details on the signup process, select the button below:     Signing Up     Once you\u2019ve finished creating your account, you\u2019ll be taken to the My TV\u00a0screen on your device. For more information on personalizing your My TV experience, select the button below:     Setting up My TV     Welcome to Sling TV!     If you\u2019d like to change your subscription, you can do so by logging in at sling.com/account\u00a0with the email address and password used when creating your Sling account.\u00a0      I\u2019m signing in to Sling TV      The next screen you\u2019ll see will ask you to sign in to your Sling TV account.          Once you\u2019ve signed in, you\u2019ll be taken to the My TV\u00a0screen on your device. Welcome back!     Don\u2019t worry, you won\u2019t need to authenticate each time you want to watch Sling TV on your device. You\u2019ll only need to authenticate after you\u2019ve been signed out of the Sling TV app.         Have additional questions?  \u00a0  Choose an answer below to see more        Is my activation code case-sensitive?      No, your activation code is NOT case-sensitive.      How long is my code active for?      Your activation code should remain active for 10-15 minutes. If your code has expired, you\u2019ll receive an error message. Back out to the landing page and select the option to sign up or sign in again to receive a new code.      How long until my device activates?      Once you\u2019ve finished signing up or signing in on your computer or mobile device, the Sling app should activate on your device within 5-10 seconds, however it may take longer. Sling does not own the networks provided on our service \u2013 we have to pay programmers for the right to offer their channels to our customers. Unfortunately, programming prices have risen, and they continue to climb with no end in sight, despite our focus on negotiating fair deals. Sling is absorbing some of the cost, instead of passing everything on to you.     While there are other options out there, Sling TV remains the best value for live sports and news, and Sling is the only service that gives cord cutters the ability to customize their TV experience at an unbeatable value.     For additional answers, choose an option below:      How do I know if my price is changing?      We\u2019re communicating with all customers via email beginning December 23rd, 2019.      How much is my price changing?      For Sling base services, you will see the following changes:   Sling Orange\u00a0is now $30/month  Sling Blue\u00a0is now $30/month  Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0is now $45/month   The 4 Extras Deal\u00a0is now $12/month for Sling Orange, Sling Blue and Sling Orange + Sling Blue subscribers.     Sports Extras\u00a0is now $15/month for Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0subscribers. Sports Extra remains $10 per month as an add-on to either Sling Orange or Sling Blue.     The Total TV Deal\u00a0is now $25/month for Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0subscribers. Total TV Deal remains $20 per month as an add-on to either Sling Orange or Sling Blue.     Any other extras you subscribe to, including Cloud DVR Plus, will remain unaffected.      When will my price change?      New Sling subscribers will see the updated price beginning December 23, 2019.     Existing subscribers will see the price change on their next bill after January 22, 2020.     Important Note:\u00a0If making changes to your subscription prior to January 22, 2020, you will be billed for the new prices listed above.     For subscribers with an account currently on pause, new pricing will take affect once the account is un-paused.     If you need to confirm your billing date, log in to your account at sling.com/account and check your auto-renew date, or get more information by selecting View Billing Details.      Am I getting more channels?      Since we launched in 2015, we have not raised the price of Sling Blue, although we have added 17 channels, the most recent being with the introduction of FOX News, MSNBC and HLN to the Sling Blue base service.\u00a0     We\u2019ve also added four networks to Sling Orange since the last price increase, in June 2018, and have grown one of the largest on-demand libraries with more than 126,000 titles across all Sling services, up from 12,000 titles at the end of 2015.\u00a0  Some of the latest features we\u2019ve launched include Cloud DVR Free, which includes 10 hours of Cloud DVR, plus the ability to record all Disney and ESPN channels, full player controls (like fast-forward and pause) across all recordable channels, a new ribbons to help with content discovery, like Trending Live and Recommended for You, as well as improved search and a binge-watching feature.     We continue to revamp the experiences across our platforms, including a refreshed UI on Apple TV and Roku devices, new guide on Roku devices, new search and micro guide on LG, Samsung and Xbox One devices, and \u2018launch into live\u2019 and \u2018browse while watching\u2019 features on Apple TV.     In the last half of 2019, Sling launched on Safari desktop, Android Chrome mobile, Facebook Portal and Google Nest Hub / Nest Hub Max \u2013 giving customers access to their favorite content on over 20 platforms.      Will this keep happening?      While we do everything in our power to fight for customers and keep prices low, we can\u2019t say if your price will change in the future. Programming prices continue to rise we no end in sight, but we work hard to negotiate fair deals that keep your prices as low as possible. Now click subscribe to activate your Sling TV service. If you have selected any extra services, you will repeat this step for each service.
